# OMNIPEDIA VOLUME 13: MASTER TEACHING REFERENCE
# 1963 languages with AI teaching signatures

---

## HOW TO USE THIS REFERENCE
When a user asks about ANY language, the AI must:
1. Find the language below
2. State its paradigm, type system, and memory model
3. Show Hello World if available
4. Compare to similar languages in the same family
5. Explain like a MASTER — not a student

---
